#!/bin/bash

# 将 stderr 重定向到 stdout，避免 execute_command 因为 stderr 输出而报错
exec 2>&1

set -e

# 获取脚本所在目录（.zscripts 目录，即 workspace-agent/.zscripts）
# 使用 $0 获取脚本路径（兼容 sh 和 bash）
SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"

# Next.js 项目路径
NEXTJS_PROJECT_DIR="/home/z/my-project"

# 检查 Next.js 项目目录是否存在
if [ ! -d "$NEXTJS_PROJECT_DIR" ]; then
    echo "❌ 错误: Next.js 项目目录不存在: $NEXTJS_PROJECT_DIR"
    exit 1
fi

echo "🚀 开始构建 Next.js 应用和 mini-services..."
echo "📁 Next.js 项目路径: $NEXTJS_PROJECT_DIR"

# 切换到 Next.js 项目目录
cd "$NEXTJS_PROJECT_DIR" || exit 1

# 设置环境变量
export NEXT_TELEMETRY_DISABLED=1

BUILD_DIR="/tmp/build_fullstack_$BUILD_ID"
echo "📁 清理并创建构建目录: $BUILD_DIR"
mkdir -p "$BUILD_DIR"

# 安装依赖
echo "📦 安装依赖..."
bun install

# 构建 Next.js 应用
echo "🔨 构建 Next.js 应用..."
bun run build

# 构建 mini-services
# 检查 Next.js 项目目录下是否有 mini-services 目录
if [ -d "$NEXTJS_PROJECT_DIR/mini-services" ]; then
    echo "🔨 构建 mini-services..."
    # 使用 workspace-agent 目录下的 mini-services 脚本
    sh "$SCRIPT_DIR/mini-services-install.sh"
    sh "$SCRIPT_DIR/mini-services-build.sh"

    # 复制 mini-services-start.sh 到 mini-services-dist 目录
    echo "  - 复制 mini-services-start.sh 到 $BUILD_DIR"
    cp "$SCRIPT_DIR/mini-services-start.sh" "$BUILD_DIR/mini-services-start.sh"
    chmod +x "$BUILD_DIR/mini-services-start.sh"
else
    echo "ℹ️  mini-services 目录不存在，跳过"
fi

# 将所有构建产物复制到临时构建目录
echo "📦 收集构建产物到 $BUILD_DIR..."

# 复制 Next.js standalone 构建输出
if [ -d ".next/standalone" ]; then
    echo "  - 复制 .next/standalone"
    cp -r .next/standalone "$BUILD_DIR/next-service-dist/"
fi

# 复制 Next.js 静态文件
if [ -d ".next/static" ]; then
    echo "  - 复制 .next/static"
    mkdir -p "$BUILD_DIR/next-service-dist/.next"
    cp -r .next/static "$BUILD_DIR/next-service-dist/.next/"
fi

# 复制 public 目录
if [ -d "public" ]; then
    echo "  - 复制 public"
    cp -r public "$BUILD_DIR/next-service-dist/"
fi

# 将测试环境数据库复制到构建产物中，生产环境直接使用这份数据库
if [ -f "./db/custom.db" ]; then
    echo "🗄️  复制测试环境数据库到构建产物..."
    mkdir -p "$BUILD_DIR/db"
    cp -r ./db/. "$BUILD_DIR/db/"

    echo "🗄️  同步构建产物中的数据库结构..."
    DATABASE_URL="file:$BUILD_DIR/db/custom.db" bun run db:push
    echo "✅ 构建产物数据库已准备完成"
    ls -lah "$BUILD_DIR/db"
else
    echo "❌ 未找到测试环境数据库文件 ./db/custom.db，无法继续构建生产包"
    exit 1
fi

# 复制 Caddyfile（如果存在）
if [ -f "Caddyfile" ]; then
    echo "  - 复制 Caddyfile"
    cp Caddyfile "$BUILD_DIR/"
else
    echo "ℹ️  Caddyfile 不存在，跳过"

File: dev.sh
Content:
#!/bin/bash

set -euo pipefail

# 获取脚本所在目录（.zscripts）
# 使用 $0 获取脚本路径（与 build.sh 保持一致）
SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"
PROJECT_DIR="$(cd "$SCRIPT_DIR/.." && pwd)"

log_step_start() {
	local step_name="$1"
	echo "=========================================="
	echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Starting: $step_name"
	echo "=========================================="
	export STEP_START_TIME
	STEP_START_TIME=$(date +%s)
}

log_step_end() {
	local step_name="${1:-Unknown step}"
	local end_time
	end_time=$(date +%s)
	local duration=$((end_time - STEP_START_TIME))
	echo "=========================================="
	echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Completed: $step_name"
	echo "[LOG] Step: $step_name | Duration: ${duration}s"
	echo "=========================================="
	echo ""
}

start_mini_services() {
	local mini_services_dir="$PROJECT_DIR/mini-services"
	local started_count=0

	log_step_start "Starting mini-services"
	if [ ! -d "$mini_services_dir" ]; then
		echo "Mini-services directory not found, skipping..."
		log_step_end "Starting mini-services"
		return 0
	fi

	echo "Found mini-services directory, scanning for sub-services..."

	for service_dir in "$mini_services_dir"/*; do
		if [ ! -d "$service_dir" ]; then
			continue
		fi

		local service_name
		service_name=$(basename "$service_dir")
		echo "Checking service: $service_name"

		if [ ! -f "$service_dir/package.json" ]; then
			echo "[$service_name] No package.json found, skipping..."
			continue
		fi

		if ! grep -q '"dev"' "$service_dir/package.json"; then
			echo "[$service_name] No dev script found, skipping..."
			continue
		fi

		echo "Starting $service_name in background..."
		(
			cd "$service_dir"
			echo "[$service_name] Installing dependencies..."
			bun install
			echo "[$service_name] Running bun run dev..."
			exec bun run dev
		) >"$PROJECT_DIR/.zscripts/mini-service-${service_name}.log" 2>&1 &

		local service_pid=$!
		echo "[$service_name] Started in background (PID: $service_pid)"
		echo "[$service_name] Log: $PROJECT_DIR/.zscripts/mini-service-${service_name}.log"
		disown "$service_pid" 2>/dev/null || true
		started_count=$((started_count + 1))
	done

	echo "Mini-services startup completed. Started $started_count service(s)."
	log_step_end "Starting mini-services"
}

wait_for_service() {
	local host="$1"
	local port="$2"
	local service_name="$3"
	local max_attempts="${4:-60}"
	local attempt=1

	echo "Waiting for $service_name to be ready on $host:$port..."

	while [ "$attempt" -le "$max_attempts" ]; do
		if curl -s --connect-timeout 2 --max-time 5 "http://$host:$port" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
			echo "$service_name is ready!"
			return 0
		fi

		echo "Attempt $attempt/$max_attempts: $service_name not ready yet, waiting..."
		sleep 1
		attempt=$((attempt + 1))
	done

	echo "ERROR: $service_name failed to start within $max_attempts seconds"
	return 1
}

cleanup() {
	if [ -n "${DEV_PID:-}" ] && kill -0 "$DEV_PID" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
		echo "Stopping Next.js dev server (PID: $DEV_PID)..."
		kill "$DEV_PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
	fi
}

trap cleanup EXIT INT TERM

cd "$PROJECT_DIR"

if ! command -v bun >/dev/null 2>&1; then
	echo "ERROR: bun is not installed or not in PATH"
	exit 1
fi

log_step_start "bun install"
echo "[BUN] Installing dependencies..."
bun install
log_step_end "bun install"

log_step_start "bun run db:push"
echo "[BUN] Setting up database..."
bun run db:push
log_step_end "bun run db:push"

log_step_start "Starting Next.js dev server"
echo "[BUN] Starting development server..."
bun run dev &
DEV_PID=$!
log_step_end "Starting Next.js dev server"

log_step_start "Waiting for Next.js dev server"
wait_for_service "localhost" "3000" "Next.js dev server"
log_step_end "Waiting for Next.js dev server"

log_step_start "Health check"
echo "[BUN] Performing health check..."
curl -fsS localhost:3000 >/dev/null
echo "[BUN] Health check passed"
log_step_end "Health check"

start_mini_services

echo "Next.js dev server is running in background (PID: $DEV_PID)."
echo "Use 'kill $DEV_PID' to stop it."
disown "$DEV_PID" 2>/dev/null || true
unset DEV_PID


File: mini-services-build.sh
Content:
#!/bin/bash

# 配置项
ROOT_DIR="/home/z/my-project/mini-services"
DIST_DIR="/tmp/build_fullstack_$BUILD_ID/mini-services-dist"

main() {
    echo "🚀 开始批量构建..."
    
    # 检查 rootdir 是否存在
    if [ ! -d "$ROOT_DIR" ]; then
        echo "ℹ️  目录 $ROOT_DIR 不存在，跳过构建"
        return
    fi
    
    # 创建输出目录（如果不存在）
    mkdir -p "$DIST_DIR"
    
    # 统计变量
    success_count=0
    fail_count=0
    
    # 遍历 mini-services 目录下的所有文件夹
    for dir in "$ROOT_DIR"/*; do
        # 检查是否是目录且包含 package.json
        if [ -d "$dir" ] && [ -f "$dir/package.json" ]; then
            project_name=$(basename "$dir")
            
            # 智能查找入口文件 (按优先级查找)
            entry_path=""
            for entry in "src/index.ts" "index.ts" "src/index.js" "index.js"; do
                if [ -f "$dir/$entry" ]; then
                    entry_path="$dir/$entry"
                    break
                fi
            done
            
            if [ -z "$entry_path" ]; then
                echo "⚠️  跳过 $project_name: 未找到入口文件 (index.ts/js)"
                continue
            fi
            
            echo ""
            echo "📦 正在构建: $project_name..."
            
            # 使用 bun build CLI 构建
            output_file="$DIST_DIR/mini-service-$project_name.js"
            
            if bun build "$entry_path" \
                --outfile "$output_file" \
                --target bun \
                --minify; then
                echo "✅ $project_name 构建成功 -> $output_file"
                success_count=$((success_count + 1))
            else
                echo "❌ $project_name 构建失败"
                fail_count=$((fail_count + 1))
            fi
        fi
    done
    
    if [ -f ./.zscripts/mini-services-start.sh ]; then
        cp ./.zscripts/mini-services-start.sh "$DIST_DIR/mini-services-start.sh"
        chmod +x "$DIST_DIR/mini-services-start.sh"
    fi
    
    echo ""
    echo "🎉 所有任务完成！"
    if [ $success_count -gt 0 ] || [ $fail_count -gt 0 ]; then
        echo "✅ 成功: $success_count 个"
        if [ $fail_count -gt 0 ]; then
            echo "❌ 失败: $fail_count 个"
        fi
    fi
}

main



File: mini-services-install.sh
Content:
#!/bin/bash

# 配置项
ROOT_DIR="/home/z/my-project/mini-services"

main() {
    echo "🚀 开始批量安装依赖..."
    
    # 检查 rootdir 是否存在
    if [ ! -d "$ROOT_DIR" ]; then
        echo "ℹ️  目录 $ROOT_DIR 不存在，跳过安装"
        return
    fi
    
    # 统计变量
    success_count=0
    fail_count=0
    failed_projects=""
    
    # 遍历 mini-services 目录下的所有文件夹
    for dir in "$ROOT_DIR"/*; do
        # 检查是否是目录且包含 package.json
        if [ -d "$dir" ] && [ -f "$dir/package.json" ]; then
            project_name=$(basename "$dir")
            echo ""
            echo "📦 正在安装依赖: $project_name..."
            
            # 进入项目目录并执行 bun install
            if (cd "$dir" && bun install); then
                echo "✅ $project_name 依赖安装成功"
                success_count=$((success_count + 1))
            else
                echo "❌ $project_name 依赖安装失败"
                fail_count=$((fail_count + 1))
                if [ -z "$failed_projects" ]; then
                    failed_projects="$project_name"
                else
                    failed_projects="$failed_projects $project_name"
                fi
            fi
        fi
    done
    
    # 汇总结果
    echo ""
    echo "=================================================="
    if [ $success_count -gt 0 ] || [ $fail_count -gt 0 ]; then
        echo "🎉 安装完成！"
        echo "✅ 成功: $success_count 个"
        if [ $fail_count -gt 0 ]; then
            echo "❌ 失败: $fail_count 个"
            echo ""
            echo "失败的项目:"
            for project in $failed_projects; do
                echo "  - $project"
            done
        fi
    else
        echo "ℹ️  未找到任何包含 package.json 的项目"
    fi
    echo "=================================================="
}

main



File: mini-services-start.sh
Content:
#!/bin/sh

# 配置项
DIST_DIR="./mini-services-dist"

# 存储所有子进程的 PID
pids=""

# 清理函数：优雅关闭所有服务
cleanup() {
    echo ""
    echo "🛑 正在关闭所有服务..."
    
    # 发送 SIGTERM 信号给所有子进程
    for pid in $pids; do
        if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
            service_name=$(ps -p "$pid" -o comm= 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
            echo "   关闭进程 $pid ($service_name)..."
            kill -TERM "$pid" 2>/dev/null
        fi
    done
    
    # 等待所有进程退出（最多等待 5 秒）
    sleep 1
    for pid in $pids; do
        if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
            # 如果还在运行，等待最多 4 秒
            timeout=4
            while [ $timeout -gt 0 ] && kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; do
                sleep 1
                timeout=$((timeout - 1))
            done
            # 如果仍然在运行，强制关闭
            if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
                echo "   强制关闭进程 $pid..."
                kill -KILL "$pid" 2>/dev/null
            fi
        fi
    done
    
    echo "✅ 所有服务已关闭"
}

main() {
    echo "🚀 开始启动所有 mini services..."
    
    # 检查 dist 目录是否存在
    if [ ! -d "$DIST_DIR" ]; then
        echo "ℹ️  目录 $DIST_DIR 不存在"
        return
    fi
    
    # 查找所有 mini-service-*.js 文件
    service_files=""
    for file in "$DIST_DIR"/mini-service-*.js; do
        if [ -f "$file" ]; then
            if [ -z "$service_files" ]; then
                service_files="$file"
            else
                service_files="$service_files $file"
            fi
        fi
    done
    
    # 计算服务文件数量
    service_count=0
    for file in $service_files; do
        service_count=$((service_count + 1))
    done
    
    if [ $service_count -eq 0 ]; then
        echo "ℹ️  未找到任何 mini service 文件"
        return
    fi
    
    echo "📦 找到 $service_count 个服务，开始启动..."
    echo ""
    
    # 启动每个服务
    for file in $service_files; do
        service_name=$(basename "$file" .js | sed 's/mini-service-//')
        echo "▶️  启动服务: $service_name..."
        
        # 使用 bun 运行服务（后台运行）
        bun "$file" &
        pid=$!
        if [ -z "$pids" ]; then
            pids="$pid"
        else
            pids="$pids $pid"
        fi
        
        # 等待一小段时间检查进程是否成功启动
        sleep 0.5
        if ! kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
            echo "❌ $service_name 启动失败"
            # 从字符串中移除失败的 PID
            pids=$(echo "$pids" | sed "s/\b$pid\b//" | sed 's/  */ /g' | sed 's/^ *//' | sed 's/ *$//')
        else
            echo "✅ $service_name 已启动 (PID: $pid)"
        fi
    done
    
    # 计算运行中的服务数量
    running_count=0
    for pid in $pids; do
        if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
            running_count=$((running_count + 1))
        fi
    done
    
    echo ""
    echo "🎉 所有服务已启动！共 $running_count 个服务正在运行"
    echo ""
    echo "💡 按 Ctrl+C 停止所有服务"
    echo ""
    
    # 等待所有后台进程
    wait
}

main



File: start.sh
Content:
#!/bin/sh

set -e

# 获取脚本所在目录

    # 发送 SIGTERM 信号给所有子进程
    for pid in $pids; do
        if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
            service_name=$(ps -p "$pid" -o comm= 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
            echo "   关闭进程 $pid ($service_name)..."
            kill -TERM "$pid" 2>/dev/null
        fi
    done
    
    # 等待所有进程退出（最多等待 5 秒）
    sleep 1
    for pid in $pids; do
        if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
            # 如果还在运行，等待最多 4 秒
            timeout=4
            while [ $timeout -gt 0 ] && kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; do
                sleep 1
                timeout=$((timeout - 1))
            done
            # 如果仍然在运行，强制关闭
            if kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null; then
                echo "   强制关闭进程 $pid..."
                kill -KILL "$pid" 2>/dev/null
            fi
        fi
    done
    
    echo "✅ 所有服务已关闭"
    exit 0
}

echo "🚀 开始启动所有服务..."
echo ""

cd "$BUILD_DIR" || exit 1

ls -lah

File: install.ts
Content:
#!/usr/bin/env bun
/**
 * Journal Design System — Component Installer CLI
 *
 * Usage:
 *   bun run cli/install.ts <component-name> [...] [options]
 *
 * Options:
 *   --all          Install every registered component
 *   --dest <dir>   Destination directory (default: ./src/components)
 *   --theme        Also copy journal CSS theme to <dest>/globals.css.journal
 */

import { mkdirSync, writeFileSync, readFileSync } from "bun:fs";
import { join, resolve } from "node:path";
import { registry } from "../src/lib/registry/index.ts";

// ─── Argument Parsing ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function parseArgs(argv: string[]) {
  const components: string[] = [];
  let all = false;
  let dest = "./src/components";
  let theme = false;

  for (let i = 2; i < argv.length; i++) {
    const arg = argv[i];
    if (arg === "--all") {
      all = true;
    } else if (arg === "--dest" && argv[i + 1]) {
      dest = argv[++i];
    } else if (arg === "--theme") {
      theme = true;
    } else if (!arg.startsWith("--")) {
      components.push(arg);
    }
  }

  return { components, all, dest: resolve(dest), theme };
}

// ─── Journal CSS Extraction ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function extractJournalCSS(globalsPath: string): string {
  const raw = readFileSync(globalsPath, "utf-8");
  const lines = raw.split("\n");
  const out: string[] = [];

  out.push("/* ── Journal Design System — Theme Tokens & Utilities ── */");
  out.push("/* Generated by the journal install CLI. Import or @import this file in your global CSS. */");
  out.push("");

  // Extract @theme inline block – journal font vars and journal-prefixed color vars
  let inThemeBlock = false;
  let themeDepth = 0;
  const themeLines: string[] = [];
  for (const line of lines) {
    if (/@theme\s+inline\s*\{/.test(line)) {
      inThemeBlock = true;
      themeDepth = 1;
      themeLines.push("@theme inline {");
      continue;
    }
    if (inThemeBlock) {
      if (line.includes("{")) themeDepth++;
      if (line.includes("}")) themeDepth--;
      if (themeDepth <= 0) {
        themeLines.push("}");
        inThemeBlock = false;
        continue;
      }
      // Keep font vars and journal-prefixed color vars
      if (
        line.trim().startsWith("/*") ||
        line.trim().startsWith("--font-") ||
        line.trim().startsWith("--color-journal-") ||
        line.trim() === ""
      ) {
        themeLines.push(line);
      }
    }
  }
  out.push("/* Journal tokens for Tailwind */");
  out.push(...themeLines);
  out.push("");

  // Extract :root and .dark journal vars with proper block tracking
  let currentBlock: ":root" | ".dark" | null = null;
  let rootJournalVars: string[] = [];
  let darkJournalVars: string[] = [];

  for (const line of lines) {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    if (trimmed === ":root {") {
      currentBlock = ":root";
      continue;
    } else if (trimmed === ".dark {") {
      currentBlock = ".dark";
      continue;
    } else if (trimmed === "}") {
      currentBlock = null;
      continue;
    }
    if (!currentBlock) continue;
    if (trimmed.startsWith("--journal-")) {
      if (currentBlock === ":root") rootJournalVars.push(line);
      else darkJournalVars.push(line);
    }
  }

  out.push("/* Journal Light Theme */");
  out.push(":root {");
  out.push("  --radius: 0.25rem;");
  out.push(...rootJournalVars);
  out.push("}");
  out.push("");

  out.push("/* Journal Dark Theme */");
  out.push(".dark {");
  out.push(...darkJournalVars);
  out.push("}");
  out.push("");

  // Extract @layer utilities block (all journal utility classes)
  let inUtils = false;
  let utilsDepth = 0;
  for (const line of lines) {
    if (/@layer\s+utilities\s*\{/.test(line)) {
      inUtils = true;
      utilsDepth = 1;
      out.push("/* Journal Utility Classes */");
      out.push(line);
      continue;
    }
    if (inUtils) {
      out.push(line);
      if (line.includes("{")) utilsDepth++;
      if (line.includes("}")) utilsDepth--;
      if (utilsDepth <= 0) {
        inUtils = false;
        out.push("");
      }
    }
  }

  return out.join("\n").replace(/\n{3,}/g, "\n\n").trimEnd() + "\n";
}

// ─── Summary Table ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function printSummary(installed: { name: string; file: string; category: string }[], themePath: string | null, dest: string, barrelPath: string) {
  // Column content widths (not including the 2-space padding on each side)
  const C1 = 20; // Component name
  const C2 = 13; // Category
  const C3 = 31; // File path
  // Slot widths = content + 4 (2 spaces padding each side)
  const S1 = C1 + 4;
  const S2 = C2 + 4;
  const S3 = C3 + 4;
  // Total box width
  const W = 4 + S1 + S2 + S3; // = 16 + C1 + C2 + C3 = 80

  const pad = (s: string, n: number) => s.length >= n ? s.slice(0, n) : s + " ".repeat(n - s.length);
  const d = (n: number) => "─".repeat(n);

  const p = (s: string) => `│  ${pad(s, W - 4)}  │`;

  console.log("");
  console.log(`┌${d(S1 + S2 + S3 + 2)}┐`);
  console.log(p("Journal Design System — Install Summary"));
  console.log(`├${d(S1 + S2 + S3 + 2)}┤`);
  console.log(p(`Destination: ${dest}`));
  console.log(`├${d(S1)}┬${d(S2)}┬${d(S3)}┤`);
  console.log(`│  ${pad("Component", C1)}  │  ${pad("Category", C2)}  │  ${pad("File", C3)}  │`);
  console.log(`├${d(S1)}┼${d(S2)}┼${d(S3)}┤`);

  for (const item of installed) {
    console.log(`│  ${pad(item.name, C1)}  │  ${pad(item.category, C2)}  │  ${pad(item.file, C3)}  │`);
  }

  console.log(`├${d(S1)}┴${d(S2)}┴${d(S3)}┤`);
  if (themePath) {
    console.log(p(`Theme:  ${themePath}`));
  }
  console.log(p(`Barrel: ${barrelPath}`));
  console.log(`├${d(S1 + S2 + S3 + 2)}┤`);
  const totalLabel = `Total: ${installed.length} component${installed.length === 1 ? "" : "s"} installed`;
  console.log(p(totalLabel));
  console.log(`└${d(S1 + S2 + S3 + 2)}┘`);
  console.log("");
}

// ─── Main ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function main() {
  const args = parseArgs(process.argv);

  // Resolve component list
  const allKeys = Object.keys(registry);
  let requestedComponents: string[];

  if (args.all) {
    requestedComponents = allKeys;
  } else if (args.components.length > 0) {
    requestedComponents = args.components;
  } else {
    console.error("Usage: bun run cli/install.ts <component-name> [...] [--all] [--dest <dir>] [--theme]");
    console.error("");
    console.error("Available components:");
    for (const key of allKeys) {
      console.error(`  ${key}  —  ${registry[key].description}`);
    }
    process.exit(1);
  }

  // Validate requested components
  const valid: string[] = [];
  const invalid: string[] = [];
  for (const name of requestedComponents) {
    if (registry[name]) {
      valid.push(name);
    } else {
      invalid.push(name);
    }
  }

  if (invalid.length > 0) {
    console.error(`Error: unknown component(s): ${invalid.join(", ")}`);
    console.error("Run without arguments to see available components.");
    process.exit(1);
  }

  if (valid.length === 0) {
    console.error("No components to install.");
    process.exit(1);
  }

  // Create directories
  const journalDir = join(args.dest, "journal");
  mkdirSync(journalDir, { recursive: true });

  // Install each component
  const installed: { name: string; file: string; category: string }[] = [];

  for (const key of valid) {
    const entry = registry[key];
    const fileName = `${key}.tsx`;
    const filePath = join(journalDir, fileName);

    writeFileSync(filePath, entry.code + "\n");
    installed.push({
      name: entry.name,
      file: `journal/${fileName}`,
      category: entry.category,
    });
  }

  // Create barrel file
  const barrelExports = valid
    .map((key) => {
      const entry = registry[key];
      return `export { ${entry.name} } from "./${key}.tsx";`;
    })
    .join("\n");

  const barrelContent = `// Journal Design System — Barrel Export\n// Auto-generated by the journal install CLI\n\n${barrelExports}\n`;
  const barrelPath = join(journalDir, "index.ts");
  writeFileSync(barrelPath, barrelContent);

  // Copy theme CSS if requested
  let themePath: string | null = null;
  if (args.theme) {
    const globalsSource = resolve(import.meta.dir, "../src/app/globals.css");
    const journalCSS = extractJournalCSS(globalsSource);
    themePath = join(args.dest, "globals.css.journal");
    writeFileSync(themePath, journalCSS);
  }

  // Print summary
  printSummary(installed, themePath, args.dest, "journal/index.ts");
}

main();

   151→          <ShowcaseSection id="content" title="Content Elements" description="Blockquotes, dividers, pull quotes, and other editorial content patterns.">
   152→
   153→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Blockquote &mdash; Default</JournalHeading>
   154→            <JournalBlockquote author="Henry David Thoreau" source="Walden, 1854">
   155→              I went to the woods because I wished to live deliberately, to front only the essential
   156→              facts of life, and see if I could not learn what it had to teach, and not, when I came
   157→              to die, discover that I had not lived.
   158→            </JournalBlockquote>
   159→
   160→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Blockquote &mdash; Ornate</JournalHeading>
   161→            <JournalBlockquote variant="ornate" author="Ana&iuml;s Nin">
   162→              We write to taste life twice, in the moment and in retrospect.
   163→            </JournalBlockquote>
   164→
   165→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Blockquote &mdash; Note</JournalHeading>
   166→            <JournalBlockquote variant="note" author="Editor&apos;s Note" source="Volume III">
   167→              The following passage was recovered from the author&apos;s original manuscript and differs
   168→              slightly from the published edition. We have preserved the original wording for historical accuracy.
   169→            </JournalBlockquote>
   170→
   171→            <JournalDivider variant="ornamental" />
   172→
   173→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Pull Quote</JournalHeading>
   174→            <JournalBody>
   175→              A pull quote extracts a key phrase from the running text and presents it prominently,
   176→              drawing the reader&apos;s eye and emphasizing the most compelling passage. It sits within
   177→              the flow but commands attention through scale and isolation.
   178→            </JournalBody>
   179→            <JournalPullQuote>
   180→              The page is not merely a surface for marks &mdash; it is a field of meaning.
   181→            </JournalPullQuote>
   182→            <JournalBody>
   183→              After the pull quote, the text resumes its measured pace, but the reader carries
   184→              the amplified words forward.
   185→            </JournalBody>
   186→
   187→            <JournalDivider variant="ornamental" />
   188→
   189→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Dividers</JournalHeading>
   190→

   192→            <JournalDivider variant="simple" />
   193→            <JournalBody className="mb-2">Ornamental</JournalBody>
   194→            <JournalDivider variant="ornamental" />
   195→            <JournalBody className="mb-2">Dot</JournalBody>

   201→
   202→            <JournalDivider variant="ornamental" />
   203→
   204→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Footnotes</JournalHeading>
   205→            <JournalBody>
   206→              The practice of marginal annotation dates back to medieval manuscripts, where scholars
   207→              would add commentary in the margins of texts<JournalFootnoteRef id="1" />. These glosses
   208→              eventually evolved into the modern footnote system we know today<JournalFootnoteRef id="2" />,
   209→              pioneered by printers in the 17th century as a way to preserve the flow of the main text
   210→              while still allowing for scholarly apparatus.
   211→            </JournalBody>
   212→            <JournalFootnote>
   213→              <JournalFootnoteItem id="1">
   214→                marginalia were particularly common in scholastic texts, where multiple layers
   215→                of commentary would be added by successive readers and scholars.
   216→              </JournalFootnoteItem>
   217→              <JournalFootnoteItem id="2">
   218→                The term &ldquo;footnote&rdquo; itself did not appear in English until the
   219→                mid-19th century, though the practice was well established long before.
   220→              </JournalFootnoteItem>
   221→            </JournalFootnote>
   222→          </ShowcaseSection>
   223→

   495→          <ShowcaseSection id="effects" title="CSS Effects & Utilities" description="Paper textures, lined backgrounds, torn edges, spiral binding, and vignette effects.">
   496→
   497→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Lined Paper</JournalHeading>
   498→            <div className="journal-lined p-6 border border-journal-rule rounded-sm mb-2">
   499→              <JournalBody className="my-0">
   500→                This text block sits atop a lined paper background, created with repeating CSS gradients.
   501→                The <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">journal-lined</code> utility adds
   502→                horizontal rules at 32px intervals. A tighter variant, <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">journal-lined-tight</code>,
   503→                places them at 24px intervals.
   504→              </JournalBody>
   505→              <JournalBody className="my-3">
   506→                The effect mimics the ruled paper found in composition notebooks and ledgers,
   507→                lending an authentic handwritten feel to digital content. Combined with a handwriting
   508→                font, the illusion becomes nearly complete.
   509→              </JournalBody>
   510→            </div>
   511→
   512→            <JournalDivider variant="dot" />
   513→
   514→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Margin Line</JournalHeading>
   515→            <div className="journal-margin-line p-4 mb-2">
   516→              <JournalBody className="my-0">
   517→                The <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">journal-margin-line</code> utility
   518→                adds a burgundy left border with extra padding, simulating the traditional red margin line found in
   519→                school notebooks and ledgers. It creates a natural visual hierarchy between the margin
   520→                area and the writing area.
   521→              </JournalBody>
   522→            </div>
   523→
   524→            <JournalDivider variant="dot" />
   525→
   526→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Paper Texture</JournalHeading>
   527→            <div className="journal-texture border border-journal-rule rounded-sm p-6 journal-vignette mb-2">
   528→              <JournalBody className="my-0">
   529→                The <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">journal-texture</code> utility
   530→                overlays subtle radial gradients that simulate aged paper stains and discoloration. Combined
   531→                with <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">journal-vignette</code>,
   532→                which adds an inset box-shadow, the result is a convincing paper aging effect.
   533→              </JournalBody>
   534→            </div>
   535→
   536→            <JournalDivider variant="dot" />
   537→
   538→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Spiral Binding</JournalHeading>
   539→            <div className="journal-spiral border border-journal-rule rounded-sm py-3 pr-4 mb-2 max-w-md">
   540→              <JournalBody className="my-0 text-sm">
   541→                The <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">journal-spiral</code> utility
   542→                adds decorative spiral binding holes along the left edge, creating the appearance
   543→                of a spiral-bound notebook. The holes repeat vertically every 80px with appropriate
   544→                left padding to keep content clear of the binding.
   545→              </JournalBody>
   546→              <JournalBody className="my-3 text-sm">
   547→                This effect works best when combined with the lined paper utility for a complete
   548→                composition notebook aesthetic.
   549→              </JournalBody>

   604→            {/* ─── Color Palette ─── */}
   605→            <JournalHeading level={3}>Color Palette</JournalHeading>
   606→            <p className="text-journal-sepia text-sm font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] mb-6 -mt-2">
   607→              Semantic journal tokens available as Tailwind classes. All adapt to dark mode automatically.
   608→            </p>
   609→            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 md:grid-cols-5 gap-3">
   610→              {[
   611→                { name: "paper", class: "bg-journal-paper", border: true },
   612→                { name: "ink", class: "bg-journal-ink text-journal-paper", border: false },
   613→                { name: "ink-light", class: "bg-journal-ink-light text-journal-paper", border: false },
   614→                { name: "sepia", class: "bg-journal-sepia text-journal-paper", border: false },
   615→                { name: "burgundy", class: "bg-journal-burgundy text-journal-paper", border: false },
   616→                { name: "forest", class: "bg-journal-forest text-journal-paper", border: false },
   617→                { name: "gold", class: "bg-journal-gold text-journal-paper", border: false },
   618→                { name: "warm", class: "bg-journal-warm", border: true },
   619→                { name: "rule", class: "bg-journal-rule", border: true },
   620→                { name: "stain", class: "bg-journal-stain", border: true },
   621→              ].map((color) => (
   622→                <div key={color.name} className="text-center">

"use client";

import React from "react";
import { registry, categories, getComponentsByCategory, getAllComponentNames } from "@/lib/registry";
import { CodeBlock, ComponentPreview, PropsTable, InstallCommand, SidebarNav, ComponentHeader } from "@/components/website/ui";

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   Journal Design System — Full Documentation Website
   Single-page app with hash routing, sidebar, live previews,
   installable code, and copy-to-clipboard.
   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ─── Hash-based router ─── */
function useHash() {
  const [hash, setHash] = React.useState("");
  React.useEffect(() => {
    const h = window.location.hash.replace("#", "") || "hero";
    setHash(h);
    const onHash = () => setHash(window.location.hash.replace("#", "") || "hero");
    window.addEventListener("hashchange", onHash);
    return () => window.removeEventListener("hashchange", onHash);
  }, []);
  return hash;
}

function navigate(id: string) {
  window.location.hash = id;
  document.getElementById(id)?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
}

/* ─── Sidebar data ─── */
function getSidebarData() {
  const staticLinks = [
    { name: "Introduction", slug: "hero" },
    { name: "Installation", slug: "installation" },
    { name: "Theming", slug: "theming" },
  ];
  const catLinks = categories.map((cat) => ({
    id: cat.id,
    label: cat.label,
    components: getComponentsByCategory(cat.id).map((c) => ({
      name: c.name.replace("Journal", ""),
      slug: c.name.replace("Journal", "").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-"),
      fullName: c.name,
    })),
  }));
  return { staticLinks, catLinks };
}

      <p className="text-sm text-journal-ink-light font-serif leading-relaxed mb-6">
        The design system uses CSS custom properties for all colors, making it fully themeable. Override any token in your <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono">:root</code> or <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono">.dark</code> selector.
      </p>

      <h3 className="font-serif text-lg font-semibold text-journal-ink mb-4">Color Palette</h3>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-3 mb-10">
        {[
          { name: "paper", cls: "bg-journal-paper", border: true, hex: "#FDFAF5" },
          { name: "ink", cls: "bg-journal-ink text-journal-paper", border: false, hex: "#2C1810" },
          { name: "ink-light", cls: "bg-journal-ink-light text-journal-paper", border: false, hex: "#5A4636" },
          { name: "sepia", cls: "bg-journal-sepia text-journal-paper", border: false, hex: "#8B7355" },
          { name: "burgundy", cls: "bg-journal-burgundy text-journal-paper", border: false, hex: "#5C1A1B" },
          { name: "forest", cls: "bg-journal-forest text-journal-paper", border: false, hex: "#2D5F3E" },
          { name: "gold", cls: "bg-journal-gold text-journal-paper", border: false, hex: "#B8860B" },
          { name: "warm", cls: "bg-journal-warm", border: true, hex: "#D4C5A9" },
          { name: "rule", cls: "bg-journal-rule", border: true, hex: "#D9CBBA" },
          { name: "stain", cls: "bg-journal-stain", border: true, hex: "#E8DCC8" },
          { name: "margin", cls: "bg-journal-margin", border: true, hex: "#C9B99A" },
          { name: "paper-dark", cls: "bg-journal-paper-dark", border: true, hex: "#F0E6D3" },
        ].map((c) => (
          <div key={c.name} className="text-center">
            <div className={`h-14 rounded-sm ${c.cls} ${c.border ? "border border-journal-rule/50" : ""}`} />
            <p className="text-[10px] text-journal-sepia uppercase tracking-wider mt-1.5 font-semibold">{c.name}</p>
            <p className="text-[10px] font-mono text-journal-sepia/60">{c.hex}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <h3 className="font-serif text-lg font-semibold text-journal-ink mb-4">CSS Utilities</h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-journal-ink-light font-serif leading-relaxed mb-4">
        Pure CSS classes for paper effects. No component import needed — just add the class to any element.
      </p>
      <CodeBlock>{`<div className="journal-lined journal-margin-line journal-vignette p-6">
  <p className="font-serif text-journal-ink-light">Notebook paper effect.</p>
</div>

<div className="journal-texture journal-vignette p-8">
  <p className="font-serif">Aged paper with texture overlay.</p>
</div>

<div className="journal-spiral journal-lined p-4 pr-6">
  <p className="font-serif">Spiral-bound notebook.</p>
</div>

<p className="font-serif journal-drop-cap">Drop cap paragraph...</p>`}</CodeBlock>

      <div className="mt-6 overflow-x-auto border border-journal-rule rounded-sm text-xs">
        <table className="w-full">
          <thead className="bg-journal-paper-dark border-b border-journal-rule">
            <tr>
              <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-semibold text-[10px]">Class</th>
              <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-semibold text-[10px]">Effect</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody className="divide-y divide-journal-rule/50 font-serif">
            {[
              ["journal-lined", "Ruled lines at 32px"],
              ["journal-lined-tight", "Ruled lines at 24px"],
              ["journal-margin-line", "Burgundy left border + padding"],
              ["journal-texture", "Aged paper stain overlay"],
              ["journal-vignette", "Inset shadow edge darkening"],
              ["journal-drop-cap", "Burgundy drop cap on first letter"],
              ["journal-spiral", "Decorative binding holes"],
              ["journal-torn-top", "SVG torn edge at top"],
              ["journal-torn-bottom", "SVG torn edge at bottom"],
            ].map(([cls, effect]) => (
              <tr key={cls}><td className="px-3 py-2.5 font-mono text-journal-burgundy font-semibold">{cls}</td><td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-journal-ink-light">{effect}</td></tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>

      <h3 className="font-serif text-lg font-semibold text-journal-ink mb-4 mt-10">Custom Fonts</h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-journal-ink-light font-serif leading-relaxed mb-4">
        The system uses three Google Fonts but is configured with CSS custom properties so you can swap them. Set <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono">--font-serif</code>, <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono">--font-display</code>, and <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono">--font-mono</code> in your <code className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono">@theme</code> block.
      </p>
      <CodeBlock>{`/* Default fonts */
--font-serif: var(--font-lora);          /* Body text */
--font-display: var(--font-playfair);    /* Headings */
--font-mono: var(--font-geist-mono);     /* Code */

/* Override with your own */
--font-serif: "Georgia", serif;
--font-display: "Garamond", serif;`}</CodeBlock>
    </section>
  );
}

/* ─── Component Doc Page (per component) ─── */
function ComponentDocPage({ entryKey }: { entryKey: string }) {
  const entry = registry[entryKey];
  if (!entry) return <p className="text-journal-sepia">Component not found.</p>;

  const installCmd = `bun run cli/install.ts ${entryKey}`;
  const componentName = entry.name;

  return (
    <section id={entry.name.replace("Journal", "").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-")} className="scroll-mt-20 py-10 border-t border-journal-rule">
      <ComponentHeader name={componentName} description={entry.description} filename={entry.file} />

      <InstallCommand command={installCmd} />

      <h3 className="font-serif text-lg font-semibold text-journal-ink mt-10 mb-4">Preview</h3>
      <ComponentPreview>
        <ComponentPreviewDemo name={entryKey} />
      </ComponentPreview>

      <h3 className="font-serif text-lg font-semibold text-journal-ink mt-10 mb-4">Source Code</h3>
      <CodeBlock filename={entry.file}>{entry.code}</CodeBlock>

      <h3 className="font-serif text-lg font-semibold text-journal-ink mt-10 mb-2">Dependencies</h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-journal-ink-light font-serif mb-6">
        {entry.dependencies.length > 0
          ? entry.dependencies.map((d) => <code key={d} className="text-xs bg-journal-paper-dark px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono mr-2">{d}</code>)
          : <span className="text-journal-sepia italic">None — fully self-contained.</span>}
      </p>
    </section>
  );
}

          {["Hand-bound leather journals with acid-free paper", "Fountain pens with archival-quality ink", "A quiet corner with natural light", "The willingness to write badly at first"].map((t) => (
            <li key={t} className="flex items-start gap-2.5"><span className="mt-2.5 w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-journal-burgundy shrink-0" /><span>{t}</span></li>

          {["Choose your medium and tools", "Set a regular time for journaling", "Begin with observations, not judgments", "Review and reflect weekly"].map((t, i) => (

          ))}
        </ol>
      );
    default:
      return <p className="text-journal-sepia italic">Preview not available for this component.</p>;
  }
}

/* ─── Tabs Demo (needs state) ─── */
function TabDemo() {
  const [active, setActive] = React.useState("prose");
  const tabs = [
    { id: "prose", label: "Prose", content: "Prose journaling is the most common form — a free-flowing narrative that captures events, thoughts, and emotions of the day." },
    { id: "poetry", label: "Poetry", content: "The poem in a journal occupies a unique space — it is neither fully public nor entirely private, a form of compressed observation." },
  ];
  const current = tabs.find((t) => t.id === active);
  return (
    <div className="border border-journal-rule rounded-sm overflow-hidden">
      <nav className="flex border-b border-journal-rule bg-journal-paper-dark/30" role="tablist">
        {tabs.map((t) => (
          <button key={t.id} role="tab" aria-selected={active === t.id} onClick={() => setActive(t.id)}
            className={`flex-1 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider font-medium transition-colors cursor-pointer ${active === t.id ? "text-journal-ink border-b-2 border-b-journal-burgundy bg-journal-paper" : "text-journal-sepia hover:text-journal-ink"}`}
          >{t.label}</button>
        ))}
      </nav>
      <div className="p-5 font-serif text-journal-ink-light leading-relaxed" role="tabpanel">{current?.content}</div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   MAIN APP
   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
export default function Home() {
  const hash = useHash();
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = React.useState(false);
  const { staticLinks, catLinks } = getSidebarData();

  /* Map hash to component key */
  const componentKey = Object.keys(registry).find((k) =>
    k.replace("Journal", "").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-") === hash
  );

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-journal-paper" style={{fontFamily:"var(--font-lora), 'Lora', Georgia, serif"}}>
      {/* Mobile top bar */}
      <div className="md:hidden sticky top-0 z-40 bg-journal-paper border-b border-journal-rule px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
        <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(true)} className="p-1 text-journal-ink" aria-label="Menu">
          <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth={2}><path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" d="M4 6h16M4 12h16M4 18h16" /></svg>
        </button>
        <span className="font-serif font-bold text-journal-ink">Journal DS</span>
        <span className="w-5" />
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-1">
        {/* Sidebar */}
        <SidebarNav
          categories={[
            { id: "general", label: "Getting Started", components: staticLinks.map((l) => ({ name: l.name, slug: l.slug })) },
            ...catLinks,
          ]}
          activeSection={hash}
          onNavigate={navigate}
          isOpen={sidebarOpen}
          onClose={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}
        />

        {/* Main content */}
        <main className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-10 lg:px-16 py-6 md:py-10">
            {/* Hero always visible */}
            <HeroSection />
            <InstallationSection />
            <ThemingSection />

            {/* Component pages */}
            <div id="components">
              {Object.entries(registry).map(([key]) => (
                <ComponentDocPage key={key} entryKey={key} />
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* Footer */}
            <footer className="mt-20 pt-8 border-t border-journal-rule pb-10">
              <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center md:justify-between gap-4">
                <div>
                  <p className="font-serif text-sm font-semibold text-journal-ink">Journal Design System</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-journal-sepia mt-1">Open source. Built with Tailwind CSS 4. Inspired by the art of journaling.</p>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-journal-sepia">MIT License</p>
              </div>
            </footer>
          </div>
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

File: use-mobile.ts
Content:
import * as React from "react"

const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768

export function useIsMobile() {
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined)

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`)
    const onChange = () => {
      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
    }
    mql.addEventListener("change", onChange)
    setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
    return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange)
  }, [])

  return !!isMobile
}


File: use-toast.ts
Content:
"use client"

// Inspired by react-hot-toast library
import * as React from "react"

import type {
  ToastActionElement,
  ToastProps,
} from "@/components/ui/toast"

const TOAST_LIMIT = 1
const TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY = 1000000

type ToasterToast = ToastProps & {
  id: string
  title?: React.ReactNode
  description?: React.ReactNode
  action?: ToastActionElement
}

const actionTypes = {
  ADD_TOAST: "ADD_TOAST",
  UPDATE_TOAST: "UPDATE_TOAST",
  DISMISS_TOAST: "DISMISS_TOAST",
  REMOVE_TOAST: "REMOVE_TOAST",
} as const

let count = 0

function genId() {
  count = (count + 1) % Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER
  return count.toString()
}

type ActionType = typeof actionTypes

type Action =
  | {
    type: ActionType["ADD_TOAST"]
    toast: ToasterToast
  }
  | {
    type: ActionType["UPDATE_TOAST"]
    toast: Partial<ToasterToast>
  }
  | {
    type: ActionType["DISMISS_TOAST"]
    toastId?: ToasterToast["id"]
  }
  | {
    type: ActionType["REMOVE_TOAST"]
    toastId?: ToasterToast["id"]
  }

interface State {
  toasts: ToasterToast[]
}

const toastTimeouts = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>()

const addToRemoveQueue = (toastId: string) => {
  if (toastTimeouts.has(toastId)) {
    return
  }

  const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
    toastTimeouts.delete(toastId)
    dispatch({
      type: "REMOVE_TOAST",
      toastId: toastId,
    })
  }, TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY)

  toastTimeouts.set(toastId, timeout)
}

export const reducer = (state: State, action: Action): State => {
  switch (action.type) {
    case "ADD_TOAST":
      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: [action.toast, ...state.toasts].slice(0, TOAST_LIMIT),
      }

    case "UPDATE_TOAST":
      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
          t.id === action.toast.id ? { ...t, ...action.toast } : t
        ),
      }

    case "DISMISS_TOAST": {
      const { toastId } = action

      // ! Side effects ! - This could be extracted into a dismissToast() action,
      // but I'll keep it here for simplicity
      if (toastId) {
        addToRemoveQueue(toastId)
      } else {
        state.toasts.forEach((toast) => {
          addToRemoveQueue(toast.id)
        })
      }

      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
          t.id === toastId || toastId === undefined
            ? {
              ...t,
              open: false,
            }
            : t
        ),
      }
    }
    case "REMOVE_TOAST":
      if (action.toastId === undefined) {
        return {
          ...state,
          toasts: [],
        }
      }
      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: state.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.toastId),
      }
  }
}

const listeners: Array<(state: State) => void> = []

let memoryState: State = { toasts: [] }

function dispatch(action: Action) {
  memoryState = reducer(memoryState, action)
  listeners.forEach((listener) => {
    listener(memoryState)
  })
}

type Toast = Omit<ToasterToast, "id">

function toast({ ...props }: Toast) {
  const id = genId()

  const update = (props: ToasterToast) =>
    dispatch({
      type: "UPDATE_TOAST",
      toast: { ...props, id },
    })
  const dismiss = () => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId: id })

  dispatch({
    type: "ADD_TOAST",
    toast: {
      ...props,
      id,
      open: true,
      onOpenChange: (open) => {
        if (!open) dismiss()
      },
    },
  })

  return {
    id: id,
    dismiss,
    update,
  }
}

function useToast() {
  const [state, setState] = React.useState<State>(memoryState)

  React.useEffect(() => {
    listeners.push(setState)
    return () => {
      const index = listeners.indexOf(setState)
      if (index > -1) {
        listeners.splice(index, 1)
      }
    }
  }, [state])

  return {
    ...state,
    toast,
    dismiss: (toastId?: string) => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId }),
  }
}

export { useToast, toast }

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

function isLiElement(child: React.ReactNode) {
  return React.isValidElement(child) && child.type === "li";
}

export function JournalUnorderedList({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <ul className={cn("my-4 space-y-2 text-journal-ink-light font-serif leading-[1.8]", className)}>
      {React.Children.map(children, (child) => {

import React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/* ─── Journal Blockquote ─── */
export interface JournalBlockquoteProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  author?: string;
  source?: string;
  variant?: "default" | "ornate" | "note";
  className?: string;
}

export function JournalBlockquote({ children, author, source, variant = "default", className }: JournalBlockquoteProps) {
  if (variant === "ornate") {
    return (
      <figure className={cn("my-8 md:my-12 text-center", className)}>
        <div className="text-journal-burgundy text-5xl font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] leading-none select-none mb-2">&ldquo;</div>
        <blockquote className="text-xl md:text-2xl font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] italic text-journal-ink leading-relaxed px-8">
          {children}
        </blockquote>
        <div className="text-journal-burgundy text-5xl font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] leading-none select-none mt-2">&rdquo;</div>
        {(author || source) && (
          <figcaption className="mt-4 text-sm text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)]">
            {author && <span className="font-semibold text-journal-ink-light">&mdash; {author}</span>}
            {source && <span className="block mt-1">{source}</span>}
          </figcaption>
        )}
      </figure>
    );
  }

  if (variant === "note") {
    return (
      <blockquote
        className={cn(
          "my-6 border-l-2 border-journal-burgundy pl-5 py-2 bg-journal-stain/30 rounded-r-sm",
          className
        )}
      >
        <div className="text-base md:text-lg italic text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-relaxed">
          {children}
        </div>
        {(author || source) && (
          <cite className="block mt-3 text-sm not-italic text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)]">
            {author && <span className="font-semibold text-journal-ink-light">{author}</span>}
            {source && <span> &middot; {source}</span>}
          </cite>
        )}
      </blockquote>
    );
  }

  return (
    <blockquote
      className={cn(
        "my-6 border-l-[3px] border-journal-gold pl-6 py-1",
        className
      )}
    >
      <div className="text-lg md:text-xl text-journal-ink italic font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-[1.75]">
        {children}
      </div>
      {(author || source) && (
        <cite className="block mt-3 text-sm not-italic text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)]">
          {author && <span className="font-medium text-journal-ink-light">{author}</span>}
          {source && <span> &middot; <em>{source}</em></span>}
        </cite>
      )}
    </blockquote>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Pull Quote ─── */
export function JournalPullQuote({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {

      className={cn(
        "my-8 md:my-10 py-4 border-y border-journal-rule",
        className
      )}
    >
      <blockquote className="max-w-2xl mx-auto text-center">
        <div className="text-2xl md:text-3xl font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-journal-ink leading-snug tracking-tight">
          {children}
        </div>
      </blockquote>
    </aside>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Divider ─── */
export interface JournalDividerProps {
  variant?: "simple" | "ornamental" | "dot" | "space" | "wave";
  className?: string;
}

export function JournalDivider({ variant = "simple", className }: JournalDividerProps) {
  if (variant === "ornamental") {
    return (
      <div className={cn("flex items-center justify-center gap-3 my-8", className)} role="separator">
        <span className="flex-1 h-px bg-journal-rule" />
        <span className="text-journal-gold text-lg select-none">&#10045;</span>
        <span className="flex-1 h-px bg-journal-rule" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (variant === "dot") {
    return (
      <div className={cn("flex items-center justify-center gap-3 my-8", className)} role="separator">
        <span className="flex-1 h-px bg-journal-rule" />
        <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-journal-burgundy" />
        <span className="flex-1 h-px bg-journal-rule" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (variant === "wave") {
    return (
      <div className={cn("my-8 text-center text-journal-rule select-none text-2xl leading-none", className)} role="separator">
        ~ ~ ~
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (variant === "space") {
    return <div className={cn("my-10", className)} role="separator" />;
  }

  return <hr className={cn("border-t border-journal-rule my-8", className)} role="separator" />;
}

/* ─── Journal Marginalia ─── */
export interface JournalMarginaliaProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  position?: "left" | "right";

export function JournalMarginalia({ children, position = "right", className }: JournalMarginaliaProps) {
  return (

      <div className="flex gap-6 items-start">
        {position === "left" && (
          <aside className="hidden md:block w-32 shrink-0 text-right">
            <span className="text-xs text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] italic leading-relaxed">
              {children}
            </span>
          </aside>
        )}
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0" />
        {position === "right" && (
          <aside className="hidden md:block w-32 shrink-0">
            <span className="text-xs text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] italic leading-relaxed">
              {children}
            </span>
          </aside>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React from "react";

/* ─── Tiny helpers for the docs page ─── */
function PropsTable({ props }: { props: { name: string; type: string; default?: string; required?: boolean; desc: string }[] }) {
  return (
    <div className="overflow-x-auto border border-journal-rule rounded-sm my-4">
      <table className="w-full text-xs font-mono">
        <thead className="bg-journal-paper-dark border-b border-journal-rule">
          <tr>
            <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-sans font-semibold">Prop</th>
            <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-sans font-semibold">Type</th>
            <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-sans font-semibold">Default</th>
            <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-sans font-semibold">Description</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody className="divide-y divide-journal-rule/50">
          {props.map((p) => (
            <tr key={p.name}>
              <td className="px-3 py-2 text-journal-ink font-semibold whitespace-nowrap">
                {p.name}{p.required && <span className="text-journal-burgundy ml-0.5">*</span>}
              </td>
              <td className="px-3 py-2 text-journal-sepia whitespace-nowrap">{p.type}</td>
              <td className="px-3 py-2 text-journal-sepia/70 whitespace-nowrap">{p.default || "—"}</td>
              <td className="px-3 py-2 text-journal-ink-light font-sans leading-relaxed">{p.desc}</td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
}

function UsageBlock({ children }: { children: string }) {
  return (
    <div className="bg-journal-ink text-journal-paper-dark/80 rounded-sm p-4 text-[11px] md:text-xs overflow-x-auto font-mono leading-relaxed my-4 whitespace-pre">
      <code>{children}</code>
    </div>
  );
}

function ComponentDoc({
  name, desc, props, usage, note,
}: {
  name: string; desc: string; props: { name: string; type: string; default?: string; required?: boolean; desc: string }[];
  usage: string; note?: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-10 pb-8 border-b border-journal-rule/50 last:border-b-0">
      <h3 className="font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-lg md:text-xl font-semibold text-journal-ink mb-1">
        <code className="text-base text-journal-burgundy/80 font-mono font-normal">{`<${name} />`}</code>
      </h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-relaxed mb-4">{desc}</p>
      {props.length > 0 && <PropsTable props={props} />}
      <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-semibold mb-1 mt-5">Usage</p>
      <UsageBlock>{usage}</UsageBlock>
      {note && <p className="text-xs text-journal-sepia italic font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] mt-3 leading-relaxed">{note}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}

function SectionTitle({ children, id }: { children: React.ReactNode; id?: string }) {
  return (
    <h2 id={id} className="scroll-mt-24 font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-2xl font-semibold text-journal-ink tracking-tight leading-tight mb-2 pb-2 border-b border-journal-rule">
      {children}
    </h2>
  );
}

              ].map((row) => (

        </p>

import React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/* ─── Journal Button ─── */
export interface JournalButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: "primary" | "secondary" | "ghost" | "link";
  size?: "sm" | "md" | "lg";
}

export function JournalButton({
  children,
  variant = "primary",
  size = "md",
  className,
  ...props
}: JournalButtonProps) {
  return (
    <button
      className={cn(
        "inline-flex items-center justify-center font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-semibold tracking-wide uppercase transition-all duration-200 rounded-sm cursor-pointer",
        /* sizes */
        size === "sm" && "text-xs px-3 py-1.5",
        size === "md" && "text-xs px-5 py-2.5",
        size === "lg" && "text-sm px-7 py-3.5",
        /* variants */
        variant === "primary" && "bg-journal-ink text-journal-paper hover:bg-journal-ink-light active:translate-y-px",
        variant === "secondary" && "bg-transparent text-journal-ink border border-journal-ink hover:bg-journal-ink hover:text-journal-paper active:translate-y-px",
        variant === "ghost" && "bg-transparent text-journal-ink-light hover:bg-journal-paper-dark hover:text-journal-ink",
        variant === "link" && "bg-transparent text-journal-burgundy underline underline-offset-4 decoration-journal-burgundy/30 hover:decoration-journal-burgundy p-0",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Input ─── */
export interface JournalInputProps extends React.InputHTMLAttributes<HTMLInputElement> {
  label?: string;
  helperText?: string;
}

export const JournalInput = React.forwardRef<HTMLInputElement, JournalInputProps>(
  ({ label, helperText, className, id, ...props }, ref) => {
    const inputId = id || label?.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-");
    return (
      <div className="space-y-1.5">
        {label && (
          <label
            htmlFor={inputId}
            className="block text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-medium"
          >
            {label}
          </label>
        )}
        <input
          ref={ref}
          id={inputId}
          className={cn(
            "w-full bg-transparent border border-journal-rule rounded-sm px-3 py-2.5 text-base text-journal-ink font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] placeholder:text-journal-sepia/60 focus:outline-none focus:border-journal-burgundy focus:ring-1 focus:ring-journal-burgundy/20 transition-colors",
            className
          )}
          {...props}
        />
        {helperText && (
          <p className="text-xs text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)]">{helperText}</p>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }
);
JournalInput.displayName = "JournalInput";

/* ─── Journal Tag / Badge ─── */
export function JournalTag({ children, className, active, onClick, ...rest }: {
  children: React.ReactNode; className?: string; active?: boolean;
  onClick?: React.MouseEventHandler<HTMLSpanElement>;
} & Omit<React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLSpanElement>, 'className'>) {
  return (
    <span
      role="button"
      tabIndex={onClick ? 0 : undefined}
      onClick={onClick}
      onKeyDown={onClick ? (e) => { if (e.key === "Enter" || e.key === " ") { e.preventDefault(); onClick(e); } } : undefined}
      className={cn(
        "inline-flex items-center text-xs font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] tracking-wider uppercase px-2.5 py-1 rounded-sm border transition-colors",
        onClick && "cursor-pointer",
        active
          ? "bg-journal-ink text-journal-paper border-journal-ink"
          : "bg-transparent text-journal-sepia border-journal-rule hover:border-journal-warm",
        className
      )}
      {...rest}
    >
      {children}
    </span>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Tabs ─── */
export interface JournalTabItem {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  content: React.ReactNode;
}

export function JournalTabs({ items, defaultTab, className }: { items: JournalTabItem[]; defaultTab?: string; className?: string }) {
  const [active, setActive] = React.useState(defaultTab || items[0]?.id);
  const activeContent = items.find((i) => i.id === active)?.content;

  return (
    <div className={cn("border border-journal-rule rounded-sm overflow-hidden", className)}>
      <nav className="flex border-b border-journal-rule bg-journal-paper-dark/30" role="tablist">
        {items.map((item) => (
          <button
            key={item.id}
            role="tab"
            aria-selected={active === item.id}
            onClick={() => setActive(item.id)}
            className={cn(
              "flex-1 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-medium transition-colors cursor-pointer",
              active === item.id
                ? "text-journal-ink border-b-2 border-b-journal-burgundy bg-journal-paper"
                : "text-journal-sepia hover:text-journal-ink hover:bg-journal-paper/50"
            )}
          >
            {item.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </nav>
      <div className="p-5 font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] text-journal-ink-light leading-relaxed" role="tabpanel">
        {activeContent}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Table ─── */
export function JournalTable({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("my-6 overflow-x-auto border border-journal-rule rounded-sm", className)}>
      <table className="w-full text-sm font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)]">
        {children}
      </table>
    </div>
  );
}

export function JournalTableHead({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <thead className="bg-journal-paper-dark border-b border-journal-rule">
      {children}
    </thead>
  );
}

export function JournalTableHeaderCell({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <th className={cn("px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-semibold", className)}>
      {children}
    </th>
  );
}

export function JournalTableBody({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return <tbody className="divide-y divide-journal-rule/50">{children}</tbody>;
}

export function JournalTableCell({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <td className={cn("px-4 py-3 text-journal-ink-light", className)}>
      {children}
    </td>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Ordered / Unordered List ─── */

function isLiElement(child: React.ReactNode): child is React.ReactElement<React.LiHTMLAttributes<HTMLLIElement>> {
  return React.isValidElement(child) && (child.type === "li" || (typeof child.type === "function" && (child.type as unknown as { name?: string }).name === "li"));
}

export function JournalUnorderedList({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <ul className={cn("my-4 space-y-2 text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-[1.8]", className)}>
      {React.Children.map(children, (child) => {
        if (isLiElement(child)) {
          return React.cloneElement(child, {
            className: cn("flex items-start gap-2.5", child.props.className),
            children: (
              <>
                <span className="mt-2.5 w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-journal-burgundy shrink-0" />
                <span>{child.props.children}</span>
              </>
            ),
          });
        }
        return (
          <li className="flex items-start gap-2.5">
            <span className="mt-2.5 w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-journal-burgundy shrink-0" />
            <span>{child}</span>
          </li>
        );
      })}
    </ul>
  );
}

export function JournalOrderedList({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <ol className={cn("my-4 space-y-2 text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-[1.8] list-none", className)}>
      {React.Children.map(children, (child, index) => {
        const number = (
          <span className="text-sm font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-semibold text-journal-burgundy min-w-[1.5rem] pt-0.5">
            {String(index + 1).padStart(2, "0")}.
          </span>
        );
        if (isLiElement(child)) {
          return React.cloneElement(child, {
            className: cn("flex items-start gap-3", child.props.className),
            children: (
              <>
                {number}
                <span>{child.props.children}</span>
              </>
            ),
          });
        }
        return (
          <li className="flex items-start gap-3">
            {number}
            <span>{child}</span>
          </li>
        );
      })}
    </ol>
  );
}

import React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/* ─── Journal Entry Card ─── */
export interface JournalEntryCardProps {
  title: string;
  date?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
  tags?: string[];
  featured?: boolean;
}

export function JournalEntryCard({ title, date, children, className, tags, featured }: JournalEntryCardProps) {
  return (
    <article
      className={cn(
        "bg-journal-paper rounded-sm border border-journal-rule p-6 md:p-8 journal-vignette transition-colors hover:border-journal-warm",
        featured && "border-l-4 border-l-journal-burgundy",
        className
      )}
    >
      <header className="mb-4">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-3">
          {date && (
            <time
              dateTime={date}
              className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-journal-sepia font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)]"
            >
              {new Date(date).toLocaleDateString("en-US", { month: "short", day: "numeric", year: "numeric" })}
            </time>
          )}
          {featured && (
            <span className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-journal-burgundy font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-semibold bg-journal-burgundy/10 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-sm">
              Featured
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
        <h3 className="font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-xl md:text-2xl font-semibold text-journal-ink leading-snug">
          {title}
        </h3>
      </header>
      <div className="text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-[1.8] text-base">
        {children}
      </div>
      {tags && tags.length > 0 && (
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-5 pt-4 border-t border-journal-rule/50">
          {tags.map((tag) => (
            <span
              key={tag}
              className="text-xs font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] text-journal-sepia bg-journal-paper-dark px-2.5 py-1 rounded-sm border border-journal-rule/50"
            >
              {tag}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </article>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Note Box ─── */
export interface JournalNoteBoxProps {
  title?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  variant?: "info" | "tip" | "warning" | "aside";
  className?: string;
}

const noteBoxStyles: Record<string, { border: string; bg: string; icon: string; titleColor: string }> = {
  info: {
    border: "border-l-journal-forest",
    bg: "bg-journal-forest/5",
    icon: "i",
    titleColor: "text-journal-forest",
  },
  tip: {
    border: "border-l-journal-gold",
    bg: "bg-journal-gold/5",
    icon: "&#10047;",
    titleColor: "text-journal-gold",
  },
  warning: {
    border: "border-l-journal-burgundy",
    bg: "bg-journal-burgundy/5",
    icon: "!",
    titleColor: "text-journal-burgundy",
  },
  aside: {
    border: "border-l-journal-sepia",
    bg: "bg-journal-stain/40",
    icon: "~",
    titleColor: "text-journal-sepia",
  },
};

export function JournalNoteBox({ title, children, variant = "info", className }: JournalNoteBoxProps) {
  const styles = noteBoxStyles[variant];
  return (
    <aside
      className={cn(
        "my-6 border-l-2 pl-5 py-3 pr-4 rounded-r-sm",
        styles.border,
        styles.bg,
        className
      )}
      role="note"
    >
      {title && (
        <div className={cn("text-sm font-semibold font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] uppercase tracking-wider mb-2", styles.titleColor)}>
          <span className="mr-2 opacity-60" dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: styles.icon }} />
          {title}
        </div>
      )}
      <div className="text-sm text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] leading-relaxed">
        {children}
      </div>
    </aside>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Figure ─── */
export interface JournalFigureProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  caption?: string;
  number?: string;
  className?: string;
}

export function JournalFigure({ children, caption, number, className }: JournalFigureProps) {
  return (
    <figure className={cn("my-8", className)}>
      <div className="bg-journal-paper-dark/50 rounded-sm border border-journal-rule/50 p-4 overflow-hidden">
        {children}
      </div>
      {(caption || number) && (
        <figcaption className="mt-3 pl-1">
          {number && (
            <span className="text-xs font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] font-semibold text-journal-burgundy uppercase tracking-wider">
              {number}
            </span>
          )}
          {caption && (
            <span className={cn("text-sm text-journal-sepia italic font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] leading-relaxed", number && " ml-2")}>
              {caption}
            </span>
          )}
        </figcaption>
      )}
    </figure>
  );
}

          </dt>
          <dd className="text-sm text-journal-ink font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)]">
            {item.value}
          </dd>
        </div>
      ))}
    </dl>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Two-Column Layout ─── */
export function JournalColumns({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (

/* ─── Journal Sidebar Section ─── */
export interface JournalSidebarProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  side?: "left" | "right";
  className?: string;
}

export function JournalSidebar({ children, side = "right", className }: JournalSidebarProps) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-8 items-start", className)}>
      {side === "left" && (
        <aside className="w-full md:w-72 shrink-0 order-1 md:order-1">
          <div className="md:sticky md:top-8">{children}</div>
        </aside>
      )}
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 order-0 md:order-2">{null}</div>
      {side === "right" && (
        <aside className="w-full md:w-72 shrink-0 order-2">
          <div className="md:sticky md:top-8">{children}</div>
        </aside>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/* ─── Journal Heading ─── */
export interface JournalHeadingProps {
  level?: 1 | 2 | 3 | 4;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
  id?: string;
}

const headingStyles: Record<number, string> = {
  1: "font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-4xl md:text-5xl lg:text-6xl font-bold tracking-tight text-journal-ink leading-[1.1] mb-6",
  2: "font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-2xl md:text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-journal-ink leading-tight mb-4 pb-2 border-b border-journal-rule",
  3: "font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] text-xl md:text-2xl font-semibold text-journal-ink leading-snug mb-3",
  4: "font-[family-name:var(--font-source-serif)] text-lg md:text-xl font-semibold text-journal-ink-light uppercase tracking-widest mb-2",
};

export function JournalHeading({ level = 2, children, className, id }: JournalHeadingProps) {
  const Tag = `h${level}` as keyof JSX.IntrinsicElements;
  return (
    <Tag id={id} className={cn(headingStyles[level], className)}>
      {children}
    </Tag>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Body Text ─── */
export interface JournalBodyProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
  lead?: boolean;
  dropCap?: boolean;
}

export function JournalBody({ children, className, lead, dropCap }: JournalBodyProps) {
  return (
    <p
      className={cn(
        "text-base md:text-lg leading-[1.8] text-journal-ink-light font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)]",
        lead && "text-lg md:text-xl leading-[1.9] text-journal-ink font-medium first-letter:text-[3.5em] first-letter:font-[family-name:var(--font-playfair)] first-letter:float-left first-letter:leading-[0.8] first-letter:pr-2 first-letter:pt-1 first-letter:text-journal-burgundy first-letter:font-bold",
        dropCap && "journal-drop-cap",
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </p>
  );
}

/* ─── Journal Lead Paragraph ─── */
export function JournalLead({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {

    <p
      className={cn(
        "text-xl md:text-2xl leading-[1.85] text-journal-ink font-medium font-[family-name:var(--font-lora)] mb-6",
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </p>
  );
}

  );

export function JournalDate({ date, className }: { date: string; className?: string }) {

    <time
      dateTime={date}

      )}
